(August 19,<div style="display:inline-block;width:4.64px">&#160;</div>2021)</div><div id="a121" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:324.707px;top:356.7px;"><div style="display:inline-block;width:4.48px">&#160;</div>&#8211;&#8211; The Cato Corporation (NYSE: CATO)<div style="display:inline-block;width:5.91px">&#160;</div>today reported net </div><div id="a140" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:384.2px;">income of $14.0 million or $0.62 per diluted share for the second quarter ended July 31, 2021, </div><div id="a174" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:411.9px;">compared to a net loss of $7.2 million or ($0.30) per diluted share for the second quarter ended </div><div id="a210" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:439.4px;">August 1, 2020.<div style="display:inline-block;width:8.9px">&#160;</div></div><div id="a217" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:475.1px;">Sales for fiscal 2020 were significantly impacted by the closure of our stores for six weeks due to the </div><div id="a255" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:502.6px;">COVID-19 pandemic, beginning March 19, 2020. Due to the impact of the unprecedented closures, </div><div id="a285" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:530.3px;">the Company will report sales compared to the past two years.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.15px">&#160;</div>Sales for the second quarter ended </div><div id="a319" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:557.8px;">July 31, 2021 were $206.0 million, or an increase of 24% from sales of $166.3 million for the second </div><div id="a358" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:585.5px;">quarter ended August 1, 2020.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.18px">&#160;</div>Compared to the same period in 2019, sales decreased 2% from </div><div id="a390" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:613px;">sales of $210.4 million for the quarter ended August 3, 2019. The Company&#8217;s same-store sales for </div><div id="a424" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:640.7px;">the quarter increased 23% compared to 2020 and decreased 5% when compared to the same period </div><div id="a457" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:668.2px;">in 2019. </div><div id="a461" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:703.9px;">For the six months ended July 31, 2021, the Company reported net income of $34.7 million or $1.54 </div><div id="a498" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:731.4px;">per diluted share, compared to a net loss of $35.6 million or ($1.48) per diluted share for the six </div><div id="a536" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:759.1px;">months ended August 1, 2020.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.17px">&#160;</div>Sales for the six months ended July 31, 2021 were $417.2 million, an </div><div id="a572" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:786.6px;">increase of 57% to sales of $265.1 million for the six months ended August 1, 2020.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.14px">&#160;</div>Compared to the </div><div id="a611" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:814.3px;">same period in 2019, sales decreased 5% from sales of $438.4 million for the six months ended </div><div id="a645" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:841.9px;">August 3, 2019.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.06px">&#160;</div>Year<div style="display:inline-block;width:1.43px">&#160;</div>-to-date same-store sales increased 56% to 2020 and decreased 7% compared </div><div id="a679" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:869.4px;">to the same period in 2019. </div></div>

<div style="padding: 7px">
<div id="Page2" style="background-color:RGB(256, 256, 256);position:relative;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;overflow:hidden;border-style:solid;border-width:thin;border-color:RGB(198, 198, 198);page-break-after:always;width:816px;height:1056px;">
<div id="a692" style="position:absolute;font-size:13.28px;font-weight:bold;left:480.093px;top:48.1px;"><div style="display:inline-block;width:288.04px">&#160;</div></div><div id="a694" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:919.3px;">8100 Denmark Road </div><div id="a700" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:937.7px;">P.O.<div style="display:inline-block;width:6.69px">&#160;</div>Box 34216 </div><div id="a706" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:956.1px;">Charlotte, NC<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.02px">&#160;</div>28234 </div><div id="a712" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:974.5px;">(704) 554-8510 </div><div id="a718" style="position:absolute;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:13.28px;left:72px;top:992.8px;">&#160;</div><div id="a719" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:63.5px;"><div style="display:inline-block;width:4.48px">&#160;</div>&#8220;Our sales were favorably impacted during the first half of the year by increased vaccination </div><div id="a750" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:91px;">availability coupled with pent-up demand, an increase in social events, summer vacation travel and </div><div id="a780" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:118.7px;">anticipated return to work for many customers, but were tempered by late merchandise shipments </div><div id="a808" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:146.2px;">driven by continued supply chain disruptions,&#8221; stated John Cato, Chairman, President, and Chief </div><div id="a834" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:173.9px;">Executive Officer.<div style="display:inline-block;width:10.22px">&#160;</div>&#8220;We anticipate seeing some impact to the business due to increased COVID </div><div id="a863" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:201.4px;">cases, however we do not expect to see the same level of impact to the business as experienced in </div><div id="a901" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:229.1px;">2020.&#8221; </div><div id="a903" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:264.6px;">Gross margin increased from 20.2% to 43.9% of sales in the quarter due to higher merchandise </div><div id="a936" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:292.3px;">margins.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.08px">&#160;</div>SG&amp;A expenses as a percent of sales increased from 26.4% to 34.5% of sales during the </div><div id="a970" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:319.8px;">quarter primarily due to increased employee benefit/bonus expense and store operating expenses as </div><div id="a996" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:347.6px;">operating hours have increased substantially compared to prior year&#8217;s phased store reopening </div><div id="a1020" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:375.1px;">following the extended store closure due to COVID. Tax<div style="display:inline-block;width:6.35px">&#160;</div>expense for the quarter was $4.6 million </div><div id="a1052" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:402.8px;">versus a $3.9 million benefit in the prior year due to the pre-tax loss.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.03px">&#160;</div>The Company ended the </div><div id="a1090" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:430.3px;">quarter with unrestricted cash and short-term investments of $216.9 million.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.08px">&#160;</div>This compares with </div><div id="a1118" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:458px;">$137.0 million for the same period in 2020.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.02px">&#160;</div></div><div id="a1135" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:493.5px;">Year<div style="display:inline-block;width:1.43px">&#160;</div>-to-date gross margin increased to 42.6% of sales from 18.4% the prior year primarily due to </div><div id="a1171" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:521.2px;">increased merchandise margins.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.01px">&#160;</div>The year-to-date SG&amp;A rate was 32.2% versus 36.4% primarily due </div><div id="a1201" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:548.7px;">to leveraging of expenses as a result of normalized sales and a $5.3 million non-cash
